GT: -alpha*v**c0 - beta*sin(x)*v - beta*sin(v) - omega0**c1*x**c2

**GT:** `-0.0884*v³ - 0.1959*v*sin(x) - 3.9977*x³ - 0.1959*sin(v)`

The GT has these basis functions: `v³`, `v*sin(x)`, `x³`, `sin(v)`.

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

### Key observations about GT:
- Contains `v³` (odd power of v)
- Contains `v*sin(x)` (product of v and sin(x))
- Contains `x³` (cubic in x)
- Contains `sin(v)` (sine of v)
- No dependence on `t`
- No polynomial terms in x other than x³
- No terms like x², x, constant, x⁵, v², v*|v|, etc.

For a candidate to match, it must be able to exactly reproduce these four terms and no others (or have extra terms that can be zeroed out).

### Critical function analysis:
- `v*exp(c*x)` cannot reproduce `v*sin(x)` for all x (exponential ≠ trigonometric)
- `v*|v|` = v²*sign(v) ≠ v³ (since v²*sign(v) = |v|*v while v³ = v*v², these are actually the same! Wait: v*|v| = v*|v|. For v>0: v*v = v². For v<0: v*(-v) = -v². So v*|v| = v²*sign(v). Meanwhile v³: for v>0: v³, for v<0: -|v|³. These are NOT the same since v²≠v³.)
- `log(c*exp(c*x + c*v) + 1)` is a softplus-like function, cannot exactly match sin(v) + v*sin(x)
- `Max(0,v)` and `Max(0,-v)`: Max(0,v) + Max(0,-v) = |v|, and Max(0,v) - Max(0,-v) = v. These give piecewise linear functions, not v³ or sin(v).
- `exp(c*v)` cannot reproduce both sin(v) and v³
